<Name>Shareef Abul-Ela</Name><date>1522332659903<//date><rating>2< /rating>< text>
I tried this Mediterranean place at the last minute and I have to say the food was pretty good. The servers were pleasant but busy.  Thry didn't have a lot of time for small talk. The place was small,  seating was a little tight but that's to be expected in a grab-and-go type of establishment like this. Honestly I walked out of there really wanting to give this place at least 4 stars or better but I have to only give it two.  I really should give it one but I'm giving it two because I don't like to bash smaller mom-and-pop establishments. The reason I scored it low was simply because not a single glove was worn by anyone behind the counter and there is no substitution for cleanliness.  I stood there and watched as the cook and the person taking the order in the person serving the food to the people seated we're touching food and knives and plastic bags without wearing a single glove on their hand.  I hope the owner of this restaurant sees this and makes that simple change it really does make a difference. I would go back once that change is made.<//text>

< Text>
Babalou's is an excellent option for cheap, (fairly) fast Mediterranean food. There are a few places I like more in San Francisco, but for Contra Costa County I'd definitely put them at the top.

Their falafel and schwarma (both chicken and lamb) are very tasty. And they have a great hot sauce. Humus is also spot on in flavor. And I really appreciate that they serve their sandwiches in a wrap versus pita - much easier to eat and tastier given it's easier to spread the flavors around.<//Text>

<rate>2< /rate>< Text>
THE WORST MEDITARIANIAN FOOD I'VE HAD!

I give them two stars because the service was fast.

We got the chicken garlic wrap, chicken plate, chicken salad, lamb gyro, lamb plate, side falafel and fries. The chicken is salty af and definitely not spit cooked. The lamb is oily but bearable. The hummus doesn't have garlic or limes. The falafel was flashed fried, the outside was dark and the inside mushy. The fries undercooked but that could be because we went during the last hour and they wanted to leave.

I personally ordered the chicken garlic wrap which was mostly bread. It had no sauce or spicy sauce, it only contained a spares amount of chicken, lettuce and tomato.

As a middle eastern, I was truly disappointed. Definitely go to The Mediterranean for legit wraps in the East Bay!</Text>

Talk about technical!!! I want to shake the person's hand who not only envisioned disc golf here but made it happen!!! My hats of to You. <rate>4</rate>< text>
This segment of the coastline along Ocean View Blvd is a favorite. The mix of rocky bluffs and small sandy coves (particularly at low tide) creates a visual feast for photography and relaxing. Sunsets along this curve of the shoreline can be spectacular and there is plenty of space for it not to feel crowded.<//text>
